 - Input IANS aadhunik jivan main zyaadaatar log vajan kam karne kii jaddojahad main lage rahete hai
 But even after many attempts, the weight is not lost
 iskaa ek ahm kaaran anheldi diet or lifestil ho saktaa he
 For example, having dinner late at night, not exercising, consuming unhealthy things, etc
 apni khanpan or rosemara kii aadaton main thode badlaav kar ke aap vajan kam kar sakate hai
 Let us know what you should pay attention to in order to gain weight and why
 
 
 
 If you want to lose weight, keep this attention -1
 junk food-aap agar vajan kam karnaa chaahate hai to aapako french friese, burgers, pizza samet sabhi aisi chizon se duuri banani padegi jinamein calories kii maatra adhik hoti he
 By consuming these things, you will not be able to lose weight even if you want to
 saath hi zyada oili chizon ke seven se metabolism kamjor hota he or fat bern nahin ho paata he
 2
 drinks-sharir main deehydration ko dur karne ke liye aapako zyada se zyada liquid kaa seven karnaa chahie
 But avoid drinking more sweet drinks, because the quantity of sugar in the body increases rapidly due to the presence of more sugar in the sweet drinks
 in drinks ke bajaae aap pani, nariyal pani, vegetable zeus or neembu pani kaa seven karen
 It has many benefits to health and weight is also under control
 3
 Taking a little break from eating - many people distance themselves from eating to lose weight quickly
 lekin bhookha rahane se vajan kam nahin hota he, balki badhata he
 Actually, being hungry weakens metabolism and does not work properly
 isse calories bern hone kii prakriya main baadha aati he
 Therefore, if you want to lose weight, instead of staying hungry, consume healthy things more
 4
 Medicines - Many people, who are troubled by their obesity, resort to medicines to lose more weight in less time
 in dawaaiyon se vajan to kam ho jaataa he, lekin sehat par bahut bura asar padataa he
 If you want to be healthy, then lose weight in healthy way
 5
 Due to the exercise-busy lifestyle, some people do not get time for exercise, then some people do not give much importance to exercise
 eksrasij ko sajaa nahin, balki majaa lekar karenge to isamen aapaki adhik ruchi paidaa hogi
 Do the right exercise to the best of your ability
 agar zyada intencity vaali eksrasij nahin kar pate hai to apane confort ke hisaab se eksrasij kar sakate hai

 Despite the 'bhagirath' efforts of various government and non-governmental organizations around the world, one in six adults in the world is illiterate and the continuing violence and poverty in various parts of the world is proving to be a major obstacle in the path of global literacy
 duniya bhar main sakshartaa ko badhaava dene vaale sanyukt raashtra shaikshanik, vaigyanik or saanskrithik sanghathan (unesco) ne is varsh 8 sitambar ko manaaye jane vaale antarrashtriya sakshartaa diwas kii vishay vastu ‘sakshartaa or shanti’ rakhaa he
 In his message on the occasion of International Literacy Day 2011, UNESCO Director General Irina Bokova said, "this year International Literacy Day has given special attention to the essential relationship of literacy and peace
 ’bokova ne kaha, ‘sakshartaa shanti kii sthapana ke liye pehali aavashyaktaa he kyonki isse kai laabh hote he

 Sri Sathya Sai Sanjeevani Hospital is the only hospital in the country dedicated to the treatment of heart diseases of children
 puri tarah nickshulk seva dene vaale is aspataal main duniya bhar se aae bacchon kaa ilaaj kiya jaataa he
 The public relations officer of the hospital, Ajay Kumar Shraf, says that this one-hundred-bed hospital was established in November 2012 and in the same year in December, a successful operation of 13-year-old girl Ritika was done
 pehle yahaan sabhi umr ke marijon ke dil kaa ilaaj kiya jaataa tha, lekin farvari varsh 2014 se ise child heart care centre ke rup main parivartit kar diya gaya, tab se yah aspataal bacchon ke dil kii dekhbhaal kar rahaa he, Shraf explains that this is a hospital with no cash counter
 matlab praathmik jaanch, oparation, ilaaj, rahanaa or khaanaa sabhi muft he
 Arrangements are made for the stay and food of two persons with children up to 12 years of age, and one person with children suffering from heart diseases between 12 and 18 years of age
 is aspataal main bacchon ke hriday rog ke 25 tarah ke aaparishan kiye jate hai
 It costs three to 15 lakh rupees in private hospitals but here it is free
 yahaan behatar doctoron kii team he jo ek din main kam se kam paanch oparation karti he
 Out of which three operations are open heart surgery
 aspataal ke jansampark adhikari bataate hai ki aspataal ke shuru hone ke baad se is varsh march maheene tak yahaan 4500 bacchon ke hriday kaa aaparishan ho chukaa he
 People from 28 states and nine other countries, including Chhattisgarh, have come here to treat their children's hearts
 shri satya sai sanjivani aspataal main fiji ke do bacchon, pakistan ke nau bacchon, bangladesh ke 11 bacchon, nigeria ke aath bacchon, nepal or srilanka ke paanch-paanch bacchon, afghanistan ke do bacchon tathaa liberia or yaman ke ek ek bachche ke dil kaa ilaaj kiya gaya he
 At the same time, a team of doctors went to Fiji and performed the operation of the heart of 26 children
 dil ke aakaar vaale 30 acre main faile is chikitsaalay parisar main satya sai saubhagyam or nursing kalege bhi he
 Sathya Sai Saubhagyam holds programs of art, culture, education and social upliftment
 ajay shraf bataate hai ki ham ise aspataal nahin balki temple aaf healing kehete hai or ise mandir kii tarah hi puja jaataa he
 The hospital rules that children who have an operation every morning are prayed for and their list is sent to millions of followers spread across the country and abroad
 jisase vah bhi prarthana main shaamil ho saken

 isliye kabhi nahin lagata ki hamen paisa kamanaa he

 Durga Puja is celebrated with great pomp, especially in Bengal, Odisha, Assam, Tripura, Manipur, Jharkhand and Bihar
 in rajyon main sharad navaratri (navratri) main shashthee se lekar dashami tak durga utsav (durga Utsav) manaaya jaataa he
 Here, Durga Utsava is also called Akalbodhan (akaal Bodhan), Shadio Pujo, Sharadotsub, Maha Pujo, Mayer Pujo, Puja or Pujo
 durga utsav ke dauraan bhavy pandal (pandal) banaakar unamem maa durga kii pratimaa sthapit kii jaati he
 During this period, apart from worshiping the mother, many colorful and cultural programs are organized
 shashthee ke din pandalon main maa durga, saraswati, lakshmi, karthik, bhagwaan ganesh or mahisasur kii pratimaaon ko sthapit kiya jaataa he
 On the day of Shatthi, the women of the house, especially the mothers, observe a fast for the well-being of their children
 saptami ke din devi pandalon kii raunak dekhte hi banati he
 On this day her favorite bhoga is offered to Maa Durga which includes khichdi, papad, vegetables, brinjal bhaja and rasgulla
 ashtami ke din bhi devi maa kii aradhana kii jaati he or unhen kai tarah ke pakwaan chadaaye jate hai
 The night of Navami is the last night of Durga Maa in the maiden
 iske baad dashami yani ki dashahara ke din subah sindur khelaa ke baad durga maa ko visarjan kar vidaai di jaati he
 During the Durga Utsav, a stage is erected in the pandal premises where colorful programs take place
 apni pratibha dikhaane kaa yah acha mauka hota he
 Various competitions are also organized during this period, especially for children

 is suvidha ke jariye sirf ek clic main duniya ke kisi bhi kone se paise transfar kiye ja sakate hai
 But if there is a slight omission, then this amount can reach the wrong person
 isliye jitani aasaani se paise duusare acount main pahunch jate hai, utani hi pareshaani hoti he waapas un paison ko clem karne main
 So take care of these things while transferring money online: -alert while adding a new beneficiary, you have to type the account number of the beneficiary twice so that the mismatch can be detected
 lekin agar pehali hi baar aapane ehtiyaat se benificiari kaa acount number likh liya he, to dobaaraa use tip karne ke bajaay copy paste kar den
 - Provide the mobile number of the beneficiary to the bank
 The mobile number of the beneficiary must also be given to the bank
 isse bank aapako or paisa jiske acount main bheja gaya yani benificiari ko mobile par tranjection kii soochna degaa
 - Do not transfer money in the cooling period; If you are sending money to a new beneficiary, then you can transfer the money only after half an hour of entering his name
 ise kooling period kaha jaataa he
